--- FILE: ./11-Scripts/proxmox/SMART/README.md ---
# Lemezállapot jelentés (S.M.A.R.T. & HDSentinel)

Ez a Bash script a szerver fizikai meghajtóinak állapotát figyeli és küldi el Gotify-ra. A cél az volt, hogy ne kelljen manuálisan ellenőrizni a logokat, hanem minden reggel érkezzen egy friss állapotjelentés a mobilomra.

## Működési elv

*  **Automatikus detektálás:** A script magától felismeri a rendszerben lévő SATA SSD-ket és NVMe meghajtókat.
*  **Aktív tesztelés:** Nem csak a korábbi adatokat olvassa ki, hanem indít egy rövid öntesztet (short test) minden meghajtón.
*  **Adatgyűjtés:** Összefésüli a smartctl short test és a hdsentinel állapotjelentő kimenetét egyetlen jelentésbe.
*  **Értesítés:** Az összeállított riportot egy POST kéréssel küldi el a Gotify szervernek, ami azonnal push értesítést generál.

### Miért hasznos?

*  **Időzített ellenőrzés:** Cron segítségével (pl. napi futtatással) automatizálható a teljes folyamat, én is ezt alkalmazom.
*  **Hiba-megelőzés:** Az öntesztek futtatásával még azelőtt kiszűrhetők a gyengélkedő szektorok, mielőtt adatvesztés történne.
*  **Központi naplózás:** Minden lemez adata (hőmérséklet, kondíció, hátralévő élettartam) egy helyen látható.

  Itt láthatom az értesítés egy részletét Gotify-on.
<p align="center">
  <img src="https://github.com/user-attachments/assets/1e7ee0e3-a313-4e9f-af83-dfee54403e0a" alt="Description" width="500">
</p>




--- FILE: ./11-Scripts/proxmox/truenas/README.md ---
# Mount Watchdog: NAS-függőség kezelés

Ez az automatizáció a Proxmox host szintjén figyeli a központi adattároló (TrueNAS) elérhetőségét. Megakadályozza az I/O várakozás miatti rendszerszintű lefagyásokat azáltal, hogy leállítja a hálózati meghajtóktól függő szolgáltatásokat, ha a NAS offline állapotba kerül.

# Főbb jellemzők

*  **Ping-alapú gyorsreakció:** A script nem vár a fájlrendszer percekig tartó timeoutjára. Amint a TrueNAS ping sikertelen, a script azonnal leállítja a függő VM-eket/LXC-ket, mielőtt azok belefagynának az I/O várakozásba.
*  **Eseményvezérelt (State Machine) működés:** A `/var/lib/mount-watchdog/nas_status.state` fájl segítségével a rendszer megjegyzi az utolsó állapotot. Ha nincs változás (pl. a NAS stabilan UP), a script azonnal kilép, így nem terheli feleslegesen a rendszert SSH logolásokkal vagy Docker műveletekkel.
*  **Aszinkron vezérlés:** A leállítási és indítási parancsok párhuzamosan futnak (`&` és `wait`), így a kritikus reakcióidő a töredékére csökken.
*  **Intelligens Boot-kezelés:** A systemd unit egy egyedi logikát használ: ha a rendszerindulás óta nem telt el 45 másodperc, törli a korábbi állapotfájlt. Ez garantálja, hogy egy Proxmox reboot után a rendszer tiszta lappal induljon, és a NAS elérhetősége esetén akkor is elindítsa a gépeket, ha azok korábban nem indultak el automatikusan.

# Kezelt technológiák és függőségek

| Típus | Azonosító / Elérési út | Művelet hiba esetén |
| :--- | :--- | :--- |
| **LXC** | 1010 (Torrent) | Konténer azonnali leállítása. |
| **VM** | 1101 (PXE/ISO) | Virtuális gép leállítása. |
| **K3s Podok** | Media Namespace | Appok (Prowlarr, Radarr, stb.) skálázása 0 példányra. |

# Rendszerkomponensek

*  **mount-watchdog.sh**: A központi Bash logika, amely kezeli a PVE (pct/qm) és a távoli K3s (kubectl) parancsokat.
*  **mount-watchdog.service**: Systemd unit, amely tartalmazza a boot-idő alapú állapotfájl-törlést.
*  **mount-watchdog.timer**: 30 másodpercenkénti ütemezést és nagy pontosságot (`AccuracySec=1s`) biztosít.
*  **Gotify integráció**: Minden állapotváltásról (TrueNAS DOWN/UP) azonnali push értesítés érkezik a mobilomra.

 Itt láthatom az értesítést részletét Gotify-on.
<p align="center">
  <img src="https://github.com/user-attachments/assets/a8a0e206-cca0-4a7e-90a7-a69804076534" alt="Description" width="500">
</p>

# 1. Containerization & Orchestration (Docker & K3s)

---

# 1. Docker and K3S

---

## 1.1 📚 Table of Contents

- [1.2 Virtualization Strategy](#vs)
- [1.3 Docker](#docker)

---

<a name="vs"></a>

### 1.2 Virtualization Strategy

Critical identity and networking layers are intentionally separated from **K3S**, running in dedicated virtual machines (VMs) and LXC containers to avoid circular dependencies.

| Hostname | Type | Stack / Role |
| :--- | :--- | :--- | 
| **ACCESS-CORE-01** | VM | **Identity:** Authentik, FreeRADIUS <br> **Access:** Teleport, Guacamole | 
| **FREEIPA-210** | VM | FreeIPA | |
| **EDGE-GW-01** | VM | Cloudflare Tunnel, Traefik | |
| **MGMT-CORE-01** | VM | Ansible, Terraform, Semaphore, GitHub Runner, management stack (Portainer) | 
| **WAZUH-SERVER-01-203** | VM | Wazuh | |
| **K3S-SERVER-01** | VM (NEW) | identity-stack (Vaultwarden), monitoring-stack (Prometheus, Grafana, Uptime Kuma), storage-stack (Nextcloud), media-stack (Sonarr, Radarr, qBittorrent, Prowlarr, Bazarr, Seerr), notification-stack (Gotify), dashboard-stack (Homarr), admin-stack (Renovate) | 
| **DNS-201** | LXC | Bind9 (Internal DNS) | 
| **UNBOUND-223** | LXC | Unbound (Recursive DNS) | 
| **ADGUARDHOME-222** | LXC | AdGuard Home (Filtering) | 
| **JELLYFIN-221** | LXC | Jellyfin (GPU Passthrough) | 
| **APT-CACHER-NG-207** | LXC | APT Cacher NG | 

---

### Failure Domain Separation

Network foundation services (DNS, gateway) and identity services run on separate virtual machines. This ensures that a Kubernetes misconfiguration or failed deployment cannot cause a full infrastructure outage (“blackout”).

---

### Infrastructure as Code (IaC)

All hosts (VMs and LXCs) are provisioned and configured using **Ansible** and **Terraform** running on the `MGMT-CORE-01` management node. This ensures reproducibility and version-controlled infrastructure.

---

### Edge Security & Connectivity

External access is provided via **Cloudflare Tunnel**, eliminating the need for exposed public ports. Internal SSL termination and forward authentication to **Authentik** are handled by a dedicated **Traefik** instance, fully independent from the Kubernetes ingress controller.

---

### Hardware Passthrough

The media stack (Jellyfin) is intentionally kept inside an LXC container. This provides simpler and more stable GPU passthrough via the host kernel compared to containerized or Kubernetes-based approaches.

---

<a name="docker"></a>

## 1.3 Docker

---

### 1.3.1 Why Docker

- **Kernel independence:**  
  With LXC, I previously encountered issues where certain services were tightly coupled to specific Linux kernel versions. After host upgrades, some services would break or require reconfiguration. Docker removes this direct dependency through an additional isolation layer, making the system more stable across kernel updates.

- **Deployment complexity:**  
  In LXC, each application must be installed manually inside the OS step by step. With Docker, prebuilt images significantly simplify the process, eliminating the need to manually resolve and install dependencies.

← [Back to Homelab main page](../README_EN.md)

# 1. Docker and K3S

---

## 1.1 📚 Tartalomjegyzék

- [1.2 Virtualizációs stratégia](#vs)
- [1.3 Docker](#docker)

---

<a name="vs"></a>

### 1.2 Virtualizációs Stratégia

A kritikus azonosítási és hálózati rétegek tudatosan a **K3S-en kívül**, dedikált virtuális gépekben (VM) és konténerekben (LXC) futnak, megakadályozva a körkörös függőségek kialakulását.

| Hostnév | Típus | Stackek / Feladatok | 
| :--- | :--- | :--- | 
| **ACCESS-CORE-01** | VM | **Identity:** Authentik, Freeradius <br> **Access:** Teleport, Guacamole |
| **FREEIPA-210** | VM | Freeipa | |
| **EDGE-GW-01** | VM | Cloudflare Tunnel, Traefik | |
| **MGMT-CORE-01** | VM | Ansible, Terraform, Semaphore, GitHub Runner, management-stack (Portainer) | 
| **WAZUH-SERVER-01-203** | VM | Wazuh | |
| **K3S-SERVER-01** | VM (ÚJ) | identity-stack (Vaultwarden) monitoring-stack (Prometheus, Grafana, Uptime Kuma) storage-stack (Nextcloud) media-stack (Sonarr, Radarr, qBit, Prowlarr, Bazarr, Seerr) notifications-stack (Gotify) dashboard-stack (Homarr) admin-stack (Renovate) 
| **DNS-201** | LXC | Bind9 (Internal DNS) 
| **UNBOUND-223** | LXC | Unbound (Recursive DNS) 
| **ADGUARDHOME-222** | LXC | AdGuard Home (Filtering) 
| **JELLYFIN-221** | LXC | Jellyfin (GPU Passthrough) 
| **APT-CACHER-NG-207** | LXC | APT Cacher NG 

### Failure Domain Separation (Hiba-szeparáció)
A hálózati alapréteg (DNS, Gateway) és az Identity réteg (Authentik, Teleport) különálló virtuális gépeken fut. Ez garantálja, hogy egy esetleges Kubernetes frissítési hiba vagy egy rosszul konfigurált YAML fájl nem okoz teljes hálózati sötétséget (blackout).

### Infrastructure as Code (IaC)
Az összes gazdagép (VM/LXC) provizionálása és konfigurációmenedzsmentje az `MGMT-CORE-01` gépen futó **Ansible** és **Terraform** segítségével történik. Ez biztosítja a reprodukálhatóságot és a verziókövetett infrastruktúrát.

### Edge Security & Connectivity
A külső elérést **Cloudflare Tunnel** biztosítja, így nincs szükség nyitott portokra a tűzfalon. A belső SSL terminálást és a **Forward Auth** irányítást az Authentik felé a dedikált **Traefik** példány végzi, amely független a Kubernetes-ben futó Ingress Controller-től.

### Hardware Passthrough
A média-stack (Jellyfin) tudatosan LXC konténerben maradt. Ez a megoldás egyszerűbb és stabilabb GPU-hozzáférést tesz lehetővé a gazdagép kernelén keresztül.

---

<a name="docker"></a>

## 1.3 Docker

---

### 1.3.1 Miért Docker

- **Kernel-függetlenség**: LXC használata mellett többször belefutottam olyan hibákba, ahol egy-egy szolgáltatás csak meghatározott Linux kernel-verzión futott stabilan. A gazdagép frissítése után a szolgáltatások gyakran megálltak vagy újra kellett konfigurálni őket. A Docker izolációs rétege megszünteti ezt a közvetlen függőséget, így a rendszer stabilabb marad kernel-frissítések után is.

- **Telepítési komplexitás**: Míg LXC-ben minden alkalmazást manuálisan, lépésről lépésre kell telepíteni az OS-en belül, a Docker-nél az előre csomagolt image-ek  leegyszerűsítik a folyamatot. Nincs szükség a függőségek egyenkénti vadászatára.

# host_vars/gepneve.yml
nfs_mounts:
  - path: "/mnt/torrent"
    src: "192.168.2.220:/mnt/ssdpool/torrent"
    opts: "nfsvers=4.1,soft,intr,noatime,rsize=1048576,wsize=1048576,timeo=50,retrans=2,_netdev,nofail"

smb_mounts:
  - path: "/mnt/backup"
    src: "//192.168.2.220/backup"
    opts: "username=rolf,password={{ smb_password }},soft,iocharset=utf8,rw,uid=1000,gid=1000,file_mode=0770,dir_mode=0770,_netdev,nofail"

  - path: "/mnt/pxeiso"
    src: "//192.168.2.220/pxeiso"
    opts: "username=rolf,password={{ smb_password }},soft,iocharset=utf8,rw,uid=1000,gid=1000,file_mode=0770,dir_mode=0770,_netdev,nofail"

--- FILE: ./13-Infrastructure_as_Code_(IaC)/ansible/roles/access_core_01/tasks/main.yml ---
# ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
# 1. KÖZÖS MAPPÁK
# ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
- name: Identity stack alapkönyvtárak létrehozása
  file:
    path: "{{ item }}"
    state: directory
    owner: root
    group: root
    mode: '0755'
  loop:
    - "/opt/app-data/identity-stack/teleport/config"
    - "/opt/app-data/identity-stack/teleport/data"
    - "/opt/app-data/identity-stack/authentik/db_data"
    - "/opt/app-data/identity-stack/authentik/config/media"
    - "/opt/app-data/identity-stack/authentik/config/custom-templates"
  
# ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
# 2. TELEPORT 
# ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
- name: Teleport GPG kulcs és Repo hozzáadása
  shell: |
    curl -fsSL https://apt.releases.teleport.dev/gpg | gpg --dearmor -o /usr/share/keyrings/teleport-archive-keyring.gpg --yes
    echo "deb [signed-by=/usr/share/keyrings/teleport-archive-keyring.gpg] https://apt.releases.teleport.dev/ubuntu {{ ansible_distribution_release }} stable/v18" > /etc/apt/sources.list.d/teleport.list
  args:
    creates: /etc/apt/sources.list.d/teleport.list

- name: Teleport telepítése APT-val
  apt:
    name: teleport=18.7.4
    state: present
    update_cache: yes
    allow_downgrade: yes

- name: Teleport adatok visszaállítása backupból (rsync)
  shell: |
    if [ -d "/mnt/backup/app-configs-backup/identity-stack/teleport/data/" ]; then
      rsync -av --no-links --exclude='*.sock' /mnt/backup/app-configs-backup/identity-stack/teleport/data/ /opt/app-data/identity-stack/teleport/data/
    fi
    sync
  become: yes

- name: Teleport config generálása
  template:
    src: teleport.yaml.j2
    dest: /opt/app-data/identity-stack/teleport/config/teleport.yaml
    mode: '0600'

- name: Teleport adatkönyvtár jogosultságok fixálása (VISSZAÁLLÍTÁS UTÁN)
  file:
    path: "/opt/app-data/identity-stack/teleport/data"
    owner: root
    group: root
    mode: '0700'
    recurse: yes

- name: Systemd service beállítása
  template:
    src: teleport.service.j2
    dest: /etc/systemd/system/teleport.service
    mode: '0644'

- name: Teleport engedélyezése és indítása
  systemd:
    name: teleport
    state: started
    enabled: yes
    daemon_reload: yes

# ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
# 3. AUTHENTIK 
# ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
- name: Authentik adatok visszaállítása (rsync)
  shell: |
    rsync -av --delete /mnt/backup/app-configs-backup/identity-stack/authentik/db_data/ /opt/app-data/identity-stack/authentik/db_data/
    rsync -av --delete /mnt/backup/app-configs-backup/identity-stack/authentik/config/ /opt/app-data/identity-stack/authentik/config/
    sync
  become: yes

- name: Authentik adatbázis jogosultságok fixálása (VISSZAÁLLÍTÁS UTÁN)
  file:
    path: "/opt/app-data/identity-stack/authentik/db_data"
    owner: "999"
    group: "999"
    mode: '0700'
    recurse: yes
  become: yes

- name: Authentik Docker Compose fájl kihelyezése
  template:
    src: authentik-compose.yml.j2
    dest: /opt/app-data/identity-stack/authentik/docker-compose.yml
    mode: '0644'

- name: Authentik stack elindítása
  community.docker.docker_compose_v2:
    project_src: /opt/app-data/identity-stack/authentik
    state: present
    pull: always
    recreate: always

# ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
# 4. FREERADIUS + DALORADIUS 
# ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

# -- Függőségek --
- name: RADIUS stack – rendszerfrissítés
  apt:
    update_cache: yes
    cache_valid_time: 3600

- name: Apache + PHP telepítése
  apt:
    name:
      - apache2
      - vim
      - php
      - libapache2-mod-php
      - php-gd
      - php-common
      - php-mail
      - php-mail-mime
      - php-mysql
      - php-pear
      - php-db
      - php-mbstring
      - php-xml
      - php-curl
      - php-zip
    state: present

- name: MariaDB telepítése
  apt:
    name:
      - mariadb-server
      - python3-pymysql
    state: present

- name: MariaDB elindítása és engedélyezése
  systemd:
    name: mariadb
    state: started
    enabled: yes

- name: FreeRADIUS, MySQL és LDAP modulok telepítése
  apt:
    name:
      - freeradius
      - freeradius-mysql
      - freeradius-ldap
      - freeradius-utils
      - git
    state: present

- name: LDAP modul symlink létrehozása (mods-enabled)
  file:
    src: "/etc/freeradius/3.0/mods-available/ldap"
    dest: "/etc/freeradius/3.0/mods-enabled/ldap"
    state: link

# -- Adatbázis alapok --
- name: RADIUS adatbázis létrehozása
  community.mysql.mysql_db:
    name: "radius"
    state: present
    login_unix_socket: /var/run/mysqld/mysqld.sock

- name: RADIUS DB felhasználó létrehozása
  community.mysql.mysql_user:
    name: "radius"
    password: "{{ radius_db_password }}"
    priv: "radius.*:ALL"
    host: localhost
    state: present
    login_unix_socket: /var/run/mysqld/mysqld.sock

# -- ADATBÁZIS VISSZAÁLLÍTÁS --
- name: Megnézzük van-e SQL dump mentés
  stat:
    path: /mnt/backup/app-configs-backup/identity-stack/freeradius/db/radius_db_backup.sql
  register: db_backup_file

- name: Létező RADIUS adatbázis visszaállítása a mysqldump-ból
  community.mysql.mysql_db:
    name: "radius"
    state: import
    target: /mnt/backup/app-configs-backup/identity-stack/freeradius/db/radius_db_backup.sql
    login_unix_socket: /var/run/mysqld/mysqld.sock
  when: db_backup_file.stat.exists

# -- VISSZAÁLLÍTÁS TAR.GZ ALAPJÁN --
- name: Megnézzük van-e tar.gz konfig mentés
  stat:
    path: /mnt/backup/app-configs-backup/identity-stack/freeradius/radius_configs_backup.tar.gz
  register: tar_backup_file

- name: FreeRADIUS, daloRADIUS és Apache konfigok visszaállítása a tar.gz-ből
  unarchive:
    src: /mnt/backup/app-configs-backup/identity-stack/freeradius/radius_configs_backup.tar.gz
    dest: /
    remote_src: yes
  when: tar_backup_file.stat.exists

# -- FreeRADIUS FRISS konfig (CSAK ha nincs sem tar.gz, sem DB mentés!) --
- name: FreeRADIUS adatbázis séma importálása (csak friss telepítésnél)
  community.mysql.mysql_db:
    name: "radius"
    state: import
    target: "/etc/freeradius/3.0/mods-config/sql/main/mysql/schema.sql"
    login_unix_socket: /var/run/mysqld/mysqld.sock
  when: not tar_backup_file.stat.exists and not db_backup_file.stat.exists

- name: SQL modul symlink létrehozása (mods-enabled)
  file:
    src: "/etc/freeradius/3.0/mods-available/sql"
    dest: "/etc/freeradius/3.0/mods-enabled/sql"
    state: link
  when: not tar_backup_file.stat.exists and not db_backup_file.stat.exists

- name: FreeRADIUS SQL modul konfig írása (csak friss telepítésnél)
  copy:
    dest: "/etc/freeradius/3.0/mods-enabled/sql"
    owner: freerad
    group: freerad
    mode: '0640'
    content: |
      sql {
              dialect = "mysql"
              driver = "rlm_sql_mysql"
              server = "localhost"
              port = 3306
              login = "radius"
              password = "{{ radius_db_password }}"
              radius_db = "radius"
              read_clients = yes
              client_table = "nas"
              mysql {
                      warnings = auto
              }
              pool {
                      start = 5
                      min = 3
                      max = 10
                      spare = 3
                      uses = 0
                      retry_delay = 30
                      lifetime = 0
                      idle_timeout = 60
              }
              acct_table1 = "radacct"
              acct_table2 = "radacct"
              postauth_table = "radpostauth"
              authcheck_table = "radcheck"
              groupcheck_table = "radgroupcheck"
              authreply_table = "radreply"
              groupreply_table = "radgroupreply"
              usergroup_table = "radusergroup"
              read_groups = yes
              read_profiles = yes
              delete_stale_sessions = yes
              group_attribute = "SQL-Group"
              $INCLUDE ${modconfdir}/${.:name}/main/mysql/queries.conf
      }
  when: not tar_backup_file.stat.exists and not db_backup_file.stat.exists

- name: FreeRADIUS config jogosultságok fixálása
  file:
    path: "/etc/freeradius/3.0"
    owner: freerad
    group: freerad
    recurse: yes

- name: FreeRADIUS elindítása és engedélyezése
  systemd:
    name: freeradius
    state: restarted
    enabled: yes
    daemon_reload: yes

# -- daloRADIUS Telepítés --
- name: daloRADIUS repo klónozása (csak ha nincs mentésből visszanyert mappa)
  git:
    repo: "https://github.com/lirantal/daloradius.git"
    dest: /var/www/daloradius
    force: yes
  when: not tar_backup_file.stat.exists

# -- daloRADIUS ALAP SÉMÁK (Csak ha egyáltalán nincs DB mentésünk) --
- name: FreeRADIUS 3 daloRADIUS alap-séma importálása (csak ha nincs DB mentés)
  community.mysql.mysql_db:
    name: "radius"
    state: import
    target: "/var/www/daloradius/contrib/db/fr3-mariadb-freeradius.sql"
    login_unix_socket: /var/run/mysqld/mysqld.sock
  when: not db_backup_file.stat.exists

- name: daloRADIUS sématisztítása és importálása (csak ha nincs DB mentés)
  shell: |
    sed -i '/INSERT INTO `operators` VALUES/d' /var/www/daloradius/contrib/db/mariadb-daloradius.sql
    mysql --skip-ssl --socket=/var/run/mysqld/mysqld.sock -u root radius < /var/www/daloradius/contrib/db/mariadb-daloradius.sql
  when: not db_backup_file.stat.exists

- name: Alapértelmezett daloRADIUS administrator létrehozása explicit módon (csak ha nincs DB mentés)
  community.mysql.mysql_query:
    login_db: radius
    login_unix_socket: /var/run/mysqld/mysqld.sock
    query: >
      INSERT INTO `operators` (`id`, `username`, `password`, `firstname`, `lastname`) 
      VALUES (1, 'administrator', '{{ daloradius_admin_password }}', 'Admin', 'User')
      ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE username=username;
  when: not db_backup_file.stat.exists

# -- daloRADIUS config fájl utólagos kezelése (csak ha NEM volt tar.gz) --
- name: daloRADIUS konfig fájl létrehozása sampleből (csak ha nincs mentés)
  copy:
    src: /var/www/daloradius/app/common/includes/daloradius.conf.php.sample
    dest: /var/www/daloradius/app/common/includes/daloradius.conf.php
    owner: www-data
    group: www-data
    mode: '0640'
    remote_src: yes
  when: not tar_backup_file.stat.exists

- name: daloRADIUS konfig – DB adatok beírása (csak ha nincs mentés)
  replace:
    path: /var/www/daloradius/app/common/includes/daloradius.conf.php
    regexp: "{{ item.regexp }}"
    replace: "{{ item.replace }}"
  loop:
    - { regexp: "\\$configValues\\['CONFIG_DB_USER'\\]\\s*=\\s*'[^']*'", replace: "$configValues['CONFIG_DB_USER'] = 'radius'" }
    - { regexp: "\\$configValues\\['CONFIG_DB_PASS'\\]\\s*=\\s*'[^']*'", replace: "$configValues['CONFIG_DB_PASS'] = '{{ radius_db_password }}'" } 
    - { regexp: "\\$configValues\\['CONFIG_DB_NAME'\\]\\s*=\\s*'[^']*'", replace: "$configValues['CONFIG_DB_NAME'] = 'radius'" }
  when: not tar_backup_file.stat.exists

- name: daloRADIUS teljes mappa jogosultságok kényszerítése
  file:
    path: "/var/www/daloradius"
    owner: www-data
    group: www-data
    mode: '0755'
    recurse: yes

# -- Apache konfigurálása és Vhost kezelés --
- name: Apache log könyvtárak létrehozása
  file:
    path: "{{ item }}"
    state: directory
    owner: www-data
    group: www-data
    mode: '0755'
  loop:
    - /var/log/apache2/daloradius/operators
    - /var/log/apache2/daloradius/users

- name: Apache ports.conf beállítása
  copy:
    dest: /etc/apache2/ports.conf
    content: |
      Listen 80
      Listen 8000
      <IfModule ssl_module>
          Listen 443
      </IfModule>
      <IfModule mod_gnutls.c>
          Listen 443
      </IfModule>

- name: Apache operators vhost konfig
  copy:
    dest: /etc/apache2/sites-available/operators.conf
    content: |
      <VirtualHost *:8000>
          ServerAdmin operators@localhost
          DocumentRoot /var/www/daloradius/app/operators
          <Directory /var/www/daloradius/app/operators>
              Options -Indexes +FollowSymLinks
              AllowOverride All
              Require all granted
          </Directory>
          <Directory /var/www/daloradius>
              Options -Indexes +FollowSymLinks
              AllowOverride None
              Require all granted
          </Directory>
          ErrorLog ${APACHE_LOG_DIR}/daloradius/operators/error.log
          CustomLog ${APACHE_LOG_DIR}/daloradius/operators/access.log combined
      </VirtualHost>

- name: Apache users vhost konfig
  copy:
    dest: /etc/apache2/sites-available/users.conf
    content: |
      <VirtualHost *:80>
          ServerAdmin users@localhost
          DocumentRoot /var/www/daloradius/app/users
          <Directory /var/www/daloradius/app/users>
              Options -Indexes +FollowSymLinks
              AllowOverride All
              Require all granted
          </Directory>
          <Directory /var/www/daloradius>
              Options -Indexes +FollowSymLinks
              AllowOverride None
              Require all granted
          </Directory>
          ErrorLog ${APACHE_LOG_DIR}/daloradius/users/error.log
          CustomLog ${APACHE_LOG_DIR}/daloradius/users/access.log combined
      </VirtualHost>

- name: daloRADIUS site-ok engedélyezése
  command: a2ensite users.conf operators.conf
  changed_when: false

- name: Alapértelmezett Apache site letiltása
  command: a2dissite 000-default.conf
  failed_when: false
  changed_when: false

- name: Apache elindítása és engedélyezése
  systemd:
    name: apache2
    state: restarted
    enabled: yes
    daemon_reload: yes

# ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
# 5. AUTOMATIKUS SNAPSHOTOZÁS A FUTÁS VÉGÉN
# ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
- name: Biztonsági mentési célmappák kényszerítése
  file:
    path: /mnt/backup/app-configs-backup/identity-stack/freeradius/db
    state: directory
    mode: '0755'

- name: Konfigurációk automatikus becsomagolása a tar.gz-be (teljes mentés)
  shell: |
    tar -czf /mnt/backup/app-configs-backup/identity-stack/freeradius/radius_configs_backup.tar.gz \
      /etc/freeradius/3.0/ \
      /var/www/daloradius/ \
      /etc/apache2/sites-available/ \
      /etc/apache2/ports.conf 2>/dev/null || true
  become: yes

- name: Adatbázis automatikus mentése helyi socketen keresztül
  shell: |
    mysqldump -u root radius --skip-ssl > /mnt/backup/app-configs-backup/identity-stack/freeradius/db/radius_db_backup.sql 2>/dev/null
    sync
  become: yes

# 2. ArgoCD sync letiltása
- name: ArgoCD automated sync letiltása
  kubernetes.core.k8s:
    kubeconfig: /etc/rancher/k3s/k3s.yaml
    api_version: argoproj.io/v1alpha1
    kind: Application
    name: "{{ item }}"
    namespace: argocd
    definition:
      spec:
        syncPolicy:
          automated: null
    merge_type: merge
  loop: "{{ argocd_apps }}"
  become: yes

# 3. Appok leállítása
- name: Appok leállítása (replicas 0)
  kubernetes.core.k8s_scale:
    kubeconfig: /etc/rancher/k3s/k3s.yaml
    kind: "{{ item.kind }}"
    name: "{{ item.app }}"
    namespace: "{{ item.namespace }}"
    replicas: 0
    wait: yes
    wait_timeout: 120
  loop: "{{ restore_apps }}"
  ignore_errors: yes

# 4. Várakozás hogy minden pod tényleg leállt
- name: Podok leállásának ellenőrzése
  kubernetes.core.k8s_info:
    kubeconfig: /etc/rancher/k3s/k3s.yaml
    kind: Pod
    namespace: "{{ item }}"
    label_selectors:
      - "app.kubernetes.io/managed-by=Helm"
  register: pod_info
  until: pod_info.resources | length == 0
  retries: 12
  delay: 10
  loop:
    - media
    - storage
    - monitoring
    - notification
    - identity
    - dashboard
    - access
    - automation
  ignore_errors: yes

# 5. Adatok visszaállítása
- name: Mappák létrehozása és rsync
  ansible.builtin.copy:
    src: "/mnt/backup/app-configs-backup/{{ item.src_path }}"
    dest: "/opt/app-data/{{ item.dst_path | dirname }}/"
    remote_src: yes
  loop: "{{ restore_apps }}"
  become: yes
  ignore_errors: yes

# 6. qbit és guacamole külön tisztítással (ezeknek kell rm)
- name: qbittorrent és guacamole célmappa tisztítása
  ansible.builtin.file:
    path: "/opt/app-data/{{ item }}/"
    state: absent
  loop:
    - media-stack/qbittorrent/config
    - access-stack/guacamole/db
  become: yes

- name: qbittorrent és guacamole rsync
  ansible.builtin.synchronize:
    src: "/mnt/backup/app-configs-backup/{{ item.src_path }}"
    dest: "/opt/app-data/{{ item.dst_path }}"
    delete: yes
    recursive: yes
  loop:
    - { src_path: 'media-stack/qbittorrent/config/', dst_path: 'media-stack/qbittorrent/config/' }
    - { src_path: 'access-stack/guacamole/db/',      dst_path: 'access-stack/guacamole/db/' }
  become: yes

- name: Renovate bot cache mappájának tiszta létrehozása
  ansible.builtin.file:
    path: /opt/app-data/admin-stack/renovate/config
    state: directory
    owner: "1000"
    group: "1000"
    mode: '0775'
  become: yes

# 7. Jogosultságok beállítása
- name: Általános jogosultságok (1000:1000)
  ansible.builtin.file:
    path: "/opt/app-data/{{ item }}"
    owner: "1000"
    group: "1000"
    recurse: yes
  loop:
    - media-stack
    - identity-stack
    - notification-stack
    - dashboard-stack
    - admin-stack
    - access-stack
    - storage-stack
  become: yes

- name: Alap chmod könyvtárakra
  ansible.builtin.command:
    cmd: find /opt/app-data -type d -exec chmod 775 {} +
  become: yes
  changed_when: false

- name: Alap chmod fájlokra
  ansible.builtin.command:
    cmd: find /opt/app-data -type f -exec chmod 664 {} +
  become: yes
  changed_when: false

- name: Gotify különleges jogok
  ansible.builtin.file:
    path: /opt/app-data/notification-stack/gotify/config
    mode: '0777'
    recurse: yes
  become: yes

- name: Nextcloud config jogok
  ansible.builtin.file:
    path: "/opt/app-data/storage-stack/nextcloud/{{ item.path }}"
    owner: "{{ item.owner }}"
    group: "{{ item.owner }}"
    mode: "{{ item.mode }}"
    recurse: yes
  loop:
    - { path: 'config', owner: '33',  mode: '0750' }
    - { path: 'data',   owner: '33',  mode: '0750' }
    - { path: 'db',     owner: '999', mode: '0700' }
  become: yes

- name: Monitoring jogok
  ansible.builtin.file:
    path: "/opt/app-data/monitoring-stack/{{ item.path }}"
    owner: "{{ item.owner }}"
    group: "{{ item.owner }}"
    recurse: yes
  loop:
    - { path: 'grafana/config',    owner: '472'   }
    - { path: 'prometheus/config', owner: '65534' }
    - { path: 'uptime-kuma',       owner: '1000'  }
  become: yes

- name: Guacamole DB jogok
  ansible.builtin.file:
    path: /opt/app-data/access-stack/guacamole/db
    owner: "999"
    group: "999"
    mode: '0700'
    recurse: yes
  become: yes

# 8. Appok újraindítása
- name: Appok újraindítása (replicas 1)
  kubernetes.core.k8s_scale:
    kubeconfig: /etc/rancher/k3s/k3s.yaml
    kind: "{{ item.kind }}"
    name: "{{ item.app }}"
    namespace: "{{ item.namespace }}"
    replicas: 1
    wait: yes
    wait_timeout: 120
  loop: "{{ restore_apps }}"
  ignore_errors: yes

# 9. ArgoCD sync visszakapcsolása
- name: ArgoCD automated sync visszakapcsolása
  kubernetes.core.k8s:
    kubeconfig: /etc/rancher/k3s/k3s.yaml
    api_version: argoproj.io/v1alpha1
    kind: Application
    name: "{{ item }}"
    namespace: argocd
    definition:
      spec:
        syncPolicy:
          automated:
            prune: true
            selfHeal: true
    merge_type: merge
  loop: "{{ argocd_apps }}"
  become: yes

  # 10. Rollout restart minden appra
- name: Rollout restart – minden namespace, minden workload
  shell: |
    for ns in $(kubectl get ns -o jsonpath='{.items[*].metadata.name}'); do
      kubectl rollout restart deployment,statefulset,daemonset -n $ns 2>/dev/null || true
    done
  environment:
    KUBECONFIG: /etc/rancher/k3s/k3s.yaml
  become: yes
  ignore_errors: yes


--- FILE: ./13-Infrastructure_as_Code_(IaC)/ansible/roles/argocd/tasks/main.yml ---
- name: Python függőségek telepítése (hogy a kubernetes modulok működjenek)
  shell: |
    pip3 install kubernetes pyyaml jsonpatch --break-system-packages || pip3 install kubernetes pyyaml jsonpatch
  args:
    executable: /bin/bash

- name: Helm ellenőrzése és telepítése
  shell: |
    if ! command -v helm &> /dev/null; then
      curl https://raw.githubusercontent.com/helm/helm/main/scripts/get-helm-3 | bash
    fi
  args:
    creates: /usr/local/bin/helm

- name: ArgoCD repo hozzáadása
  kubernetes.core.helm_repository:
    name: argo
    repo_url: "https://argoproj.github.io/argo-helm"
  environment:
    PATH: "{{ ansible_env.PATH }}:/usr/local/bin"

- name: ArgoCD telepítése és jelszó/port konfigurálása
  kubernetes.core.helm:
    name: argocd
    chart_ref: argo/argo-cd
    release_namespace: argocd
    create_namespace: true
    kubeconfig: /etc/rancher/k3s/k3s.yaml
    binary_path: /usr/local/bin/helm
    wait: yes
    values:
      server:
        service:
          type: NodePort
          ports:
            - name: https
              port: 443
              targetPort: 8080
              nodePort: 30007 
      configs:
        secret:
          argocd.admin.password: '{{ argocd_admin_pwd_hash }}'
          # Kényszerítjük a frissítést az aktuális idővel
          argocd.admin.passwordMtime: "{{ lookup('pipe', 'date -u +%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%SZ') }}"

- name: Kényszerített port és jelszó felülírás (Patch), ha a Helm nem vinné át
  shell: |
    kubectl -n argocd patch svc argocd-server -p '{"spec": {"type": "NodePort", "ports": [{"name": "https", "port": 443, "targetPort": 8080, "nodePort": 30007}]}}' --type=merge || true
    kubectl -n argocd patch secret argocd-secret -p '{"stringData": {"admin.password": "{{ argocd_admin_pwd_hash }}", "admin.passwordMtime": "'$(date +%FT%T%Z)'"}}' --type=merge || true
- name: ArgoCD szerver újraindítása az új jelszó érvényesítéséhez
  shell: kubectl rollout restart deployment argocd-server -n argocd


--- FILE: ./13-Infrastructure_as_Code_(IaC)/ansible/roles/argocd_apps/tasks/main.yml ---
# Ez a feladat hozza létre az ArgoCD "Application" objektumokat. 
# Összeköti a GitHub repó adott mappáit (pl. kubernetes/apps/media) 
# a K3s névtéreivel (pl. media namespace), és bekapcsolja az automatikus szinkronizációt.
---
- name: GitHub Privát Repo hitelesítés (Secret)
  kubernetes.core.k8s:
    kubeconfig: /etc/rancher/k3s/k3s.yaml
    state: present
    definition:
      apiVersion: v1
      kind: Secret
      metadata:
        name: github-repo-auth
        namespace: argocd
        labels:
          argocd.argoproj.io/secret-type: repository
      stringData:
        type: git
        url: "https://github.com/torokrolf/homelab-infra.git"
        username: "torokrolf"
        password: '{{ github_pat_argocd }}'

- name: ArgoCD Application-ök létrehozása (Összes Stack)
  kubernetes.core.k8s:
    kubeconfig: /etc/rancher/k3s/k3s.yaml
    state: present
    definition:
      apiVersion: argoproj.io/v1alpha1
      kind: Application
      metadata:
        name: "{{ item.name }}"
        namespace: argocd
      spec:
        project: default
        source:
          repoURL: 'https://github.com/torokrolf/homelab-infra.git'
          targetRevision: HEAD
          path: "{{ item.path }}"
          directory:
            recurse: true
        destination:
          server: 'https://kubernetes.default.svc'
          namespace: "{{ item.namespace }}"
        syncPolicy:
          automated: { prune: true, selfHeal: true }
          syncOptions: [ CreateNamespace=true ]
  loop:
    - { name: 'media-stack', path: 'kubernetes/apps/media', namespace: 'media' }
    - { name: 'storage-stack', path: 'kubernetes/apps/storage', namespace: 'storage' }
    - { name: 'monitoring-stack', path: 'kubernetes/apps/monitoring', namespace: 'monitoring' }
    - { name: 'notification-stack', path: 'kubernetes/apps/notification', namespace: 'notification' }
    - { name: 'identity-stack', path: 'kubernetes/apps/identity', namespace: 'identity' }
    - { name: 'automation-stack', path: 'kubernetes/apps/automation', namespace: 'automation' }
    - { name: 'dashboard-stack', path: 'kubernetes/apps/dashboard', namespace: 'dashboard' }
    - { name: 'access-stack', path: 'kubernetes/apps/access', namespace: 'access' }

- name: Várakozás a rollout elindulására (45 mp)
  pause:
    seconds: 45


--- FILE: ./13-Infrastructure_as_Code_(IaC)/ansible/roles/backup/tasks/access_core.yml ---
- name: Docker konténerek leállítása
  shell: docker stop $(docker ps -q) 2>/dev/null || true

- name: /opt/app-data rsync mentése (Dátumozott mappába)
  shell: |
    rsync -avzhL --exclude="*.sock" /opt/app-data/ /mnt/backup/app-configs-backup-{{ ansible_date_time.date }}/
  args:
    executable: /bin/bash

- name: Docker konténerek visszaindítása
  shell: docker start $(docker ps -a -q) 2>/dev/null || true

- name: FreeRADIUS mentési mappa létrehozása (Most már a dátumozott mappán belül!)
  file:
    path: "/mnt/backup/app-configs-backup-{{ ansible_date_time.date }}/identity-stack/freeradius/db"
    state: directory
    mode: '0755'

- name: FreeRADIUS / daloRADIUS / Apache konfigok becsomagolása
  shell: |
    tar -czf /mnt/backup/app-configs-backup-{{ ansible_date_time.date }}/identity-stack/freeradius/radius_configs_backup.tar.gz \
      /etc/freeradius/3.0/ \
      /var/www/daloradius/ \
      /etc/apache2/sites-available/ \
      /etc/apache2/ports.conf 2>/dev/null || true
  args:
    executable: /bin/bash

- name: RADIUS adatbázis mentése (mysqldump)
  shell: |
    mysqldump -u root radius --skip-ssl > /mnt/backup/app-configs-backup-{{ ansible_date_time.date }}/identity-stack/freeradius/db/radius_db_backup.sql 2>/dev/null
    sync
  args:
    executable: /bin/bash


--- FILE: ./13-Infrastructure_as_Code_(IaC)/ansible/roles/backup/tasks/edge_gw.yml ---
---
- name: Docker konténerek leállítása
  shell: docker stop $(docker ps -q) 2>/dev/null || true

- name: /opt/app-data rsync mentése
  shell: |
    rsync -avzh /opt/app-data/ /mnt/backup/app-configs-backup-$(date +%F)/
  args:
    executable: /bin/bash

- name: Docker konténerek visszaindítása
  shell: docker start $(docker ps -a -q) 2>/dev/null || true


--- FILE: ./13-Infrastructure_as_Code_(IaC)/ansible/roles/backup/tasks/k3s_server.yml ---
---
- name: App namespace-ek összegyűjtése (rendszer-namespace-ek nélkül)
  shell: |
    kubectl get ns --no-headers -o custom-columns=NAME:.metadata.name | grep -Ev '^(kube-system|kube-public|kube-node-lease)$'
  register: k3s_namespaces
  changed_when: false
  args:
    executable: /bin/bash

- name: Deploymentek és StatefulSetek leállítása (replicas=0)
  shell: |
    for ns in {{ k3s_namespaces.stdout_lines | join(' ') }}; do
      kubectl scale deployment,statefulset --all --replicas=0 -n $ns || true
    done
  args:
    executable: /bin/bash

- name: Podok teljes leállásának megvárása
  shell: |
    for ns in {{ k3s_namespaces.stdout_lines | join(' ') }}; do
      kubectl wait --for=delete pod --all -n $ns --timeout=60s 2>/dev/null || true
    done
  args:
    executable: /bin/bash

- name: /opt/app-data rsync mentése
  shell: |
    rsync -avzh --exclude="*.sock" --exclude="admin-stack/" /opt/app-data/ /mnt/backup/app-configs-backup-$(date +%F)/
  args:
    executable: /bin/bash

- name: Deploymentek és StatefulSetek visszaindítása (replicas=1)
  shell: |
    for ns in {{ k3s_namespaces.stdout_lines | join(' ') }}; do
      kubectl scale deployment,statefulset --all --replicas=1 -n $ns || true
    done
  args:
    executable: /bin/bash

- name: Megvárjuk, amíg az appok (és a Gotify) ténylegesen elindulnak (Ready)
  shell: |
    for ns in {{ k3s_namespaces.stdout_lines | join(' ') }}; do
      kubectl wait --for=condition=Ready pod --all -n $ns --timeout=90s 2>/dev/null || true
    done
  args:
    executable: /bin/bash

--- FILE: ./13-Infrastructure_as_Code_(IaC)/ansible/roles/common/tasks/main.yml ---
# 1. APT PROXY BEÁLLÍTÁSA
- name: Set APT proxy
  copy:
    dest: /etc/apt/apt.conf.d/01proxy
    content: |
      Acquire::http::Proxy "http://192.168.2.207:3142";
    owner: root
    group: root
    mode: '0644'
  when: ansible_host != "192.168.2.207"

# 2. ALAPCSOMAGOK TELEPÍTÉSE
- name: Alapcsomagok, MC és Node Exporter telepítése
  tags: [programtelepitesek]
  apt:
    name:
      - python3
      - python3-pip
      - curl
      - git
      - mc
      - prometheus-node-exporter
    state: present
    update_cache: yes
    cache_valid_time: 3600
  register: apt_result
  until: apt_result is success
  retries: 3
  delay: 5
  become: yes
  async: 600
  poll: 10

# 3. FELHASZNÁLÓ ÉS SSH BEÁLLÍTÁSOK
- name: "{{ target_username }} felhasználó beállítása"
  user:
    name: "{{ target_username }}"
    shell: /bin/bash
    groups: sudo
    append: yes
    password: "{{ target_password_hash }}"

- name: SSH kulcsok felmásolása
  authorized_key:
    user: "{{ target_username }}"
    key: "{{ item }}"
  loop: "{{ ssh_public_keys }}"

- name: SSH Hardening és Banner
  lineinfile:
    path: /etc/ssh/sshd_config
    regexp: "{{ item.reg }}"
    line: "{{ item.line }}"
  loop:
    - { reg: '^#?PermitRootLogin',        line: 'PermitRootLogin no' }
    - { reg: '^#?PasswordAuthentication', line: 'PasswordAuthentication no' }
    - { reg: '^#?PubkeyAuthentication',   line: 'PubkeyAuthentication yes' }
    - { reg: '^#?Banner',                 line: 'Banner /etc/issue.net' }
  notify: Restart SSH

- name: Jogi figyelmeztetes (Banner) beallitasa
  copy:
    dest: /etc/issue.net
    content: "FIGYELEM! Csak jogosult felhasznaloknak! Minden tevekenyseg naplozva van.\n"

- name: Shell Timeout (TMOUT)
  lineinfile:
    path: /etc/profile
    regexp: '^export TMOUT='
    line: 'export TMOUT=900'

# 4. IDŐZÓNA
- name: Rendszer időzóna beállítása
  community.general.timezone:
    name: "{{ system_timezone }}"

# 5. PROMETHEUS NODE EXPORTER
- name: Node Exporter inditasa es engedelyezese
  systemd:
    name: prometheus-node-exporter
    state: started
    enabled: yes

# 6. REBOOT ELLENŐRZÉS
- name: Reboot ellenőrzése
  stat:
    path: /var/run/reboot-required
  register: reboot_required
  notify: "Rendszer ujrainditasa"


--- FILE: ./13-Infrastructure_as_Code_(IaC)/ansible/roles/docker/tasks/main.yml ---
---
- name: Docker függőségek telepítése
  apt:
    name: [curl, gnupg, lsb-release, ca-certificates]
    state: present

- name: Docker GPG kulcs és Repo beállítása
  block:
    - name: GPG könyvtár létrehozása
      file: { path: /etc/apt/keyrings, state: directory, mode: '0755' }
    - name: GPG kulcs letöltése
      apt_key:
        url: https://download.docker.com/linux/ubuntu/gpg
        keyring: /etc/apt/keyrings/docker.gpg
    - name: Repo hozzáadása
      apt_repository:
        repo: "deb [arch=amd64 signed-by=/etc/apt/keyrings/docker.gpg] https://download.docker.com/linux/ubuntu {{ ansible_distribution_release }} stable"
        filename: docker

- name: Docker csomagok telepítése
  apt:
    name: [docker-ce, docker-ce-cli, containerd.io, docker-compose-plugin]
    state: present
    update_cache: yes

--- FILE: ./13-Infrastructure_as_Code_(IaC)/ansible/roles/k3s_setup/tasks/main.yml ---
---
# ==============================================================================
# 1. FÁZIS: OS ELŐKÉSZÍTÉS
# ==============================================================================

# --- SWAP ---
# A Kubernetes/K3s nem szereti, ha a Linux elkezdi a memóriát a lassú lemezre (swap) dobálni.
- name: Disable SWAP immediately
  command: swapoff -a
  when: ansible_swaptotal_mb > 0 
  tags: swap

# Hiába kapcsoljuk ki, reboot után visszajönne. Itt kikommenteljük az fstab fájlból véglegesen.
- name: Remove SWAP from fstab
  replace:
    path: /etc/fstab
    regexp: '^([^#].*?\sswap\s+.*)$'
    replace: '# \1'
  tags: swap

# --- KERNEL MODULOK ELŐKÉSZÍTÉSE ---
- name: Create /etc/modules-load.d/k3s.conf
  copy:
    dest: /etc/modules-load.d/k3s.conf
    content: |
      overlay      
      br_netfilter 
  register: modules_conf

- name: Load kernel modules
  modprobe:
    name: "{{ item }}"
    state: present
  loop:
    - overlay
    - br_netfilter

# --- HÁLÓZATI ÚTVONALVÁLASZTÁS ÉS TŰZFAL ---
- name: Set sysctl parameters for K3s
  sysctl:
    name: "{{ item.key }}"
    value: "{{ item.value }}"
    state: present
    sysctl_file: /etc/sysctl.d/99-k3s.conf
    reload: yes
  loop:
    - { key: 'net.bridge.bridge-nf-call-iptables', value: '1' }
    - { key: 'net.bridge.bridge-nf-call-ip6tables', value: '1' }
    - { key: 'net.ipv4.ip_forward', value: '1' }


# ==============================================================================
# 2. FÁZIS: K3S TELEPÍTÉS ÉS INICIALIZÁLÁS
# ==============================================================================

- name: K3s telepítése (Master init)
  shell: |
    curl -sfL https://get.k3s.io | sh -s - server \
    --cluster-init \
    --write-kubeconfig-mode 644 \
    --disable servicelb \
    --disable traefik
  args:
    creates: /usr/local/bin/k3s 

- name: Kubeconfig mentése változóba (később jól jöhet)
  slurp:
    src: /etc/rancher/k3s/k3s.yaml
  register: kubeconfig_raw

# ==============================================================================
# 3. FÁZIS: K9S TELEPÍTÉS
# ==============================================================================
- name: k9s telepítése
  vars:
    k9s_version: "v0.32.7"
  block:
    - name: k9s letöltése
      get_url:
        url: "https://github.com/derailed/k9s/releases/download/{{ k9s_version }}/k9s_Linux_amd64.tar.gz"
        dest: /tmp/k9s.tar.gz
        mode: '0644'

    - name: k9s kicsomagolása
      unarchive:
        src: /tmp/k9s.tar.gz
        dest: /tmp
        remote_src: yes

    - name: k9s bináris másolása
      copy:
        src: /tmp/k9s
        dest: /usr/local/bin/k9s
        mode: '0755'
        remote_src: yes

    - name: Temp fájlok törlése
      file:
        path: "{{ item }}"
        state: absent
      loop:
        - /tmp/k9s.tar.gz
        - /tmp/k9s

    - name: KUBECONFIG beállítása bashrc-ben
      lineinfile:
        path: /root/.bashrc
        line: 'export KUBECONFIG=/etc/rancher/k3s/k3s.yaml'
        state: present


--- FILE: ./13-Infrastructure_as_Code_(IaC)/ansible/roles/mounts/tasks/main.yml ---
---
- name: Kliens csomagok telepítése
  become: yes
  apt:
    name: ["nfs-common", "cifs-utils"]
    state: present

- name: Mount pontok létezésének ellenőrzése
  stat:
    path: "{{ item.path }}"
  register: mount_stat
  loop: "{{ nfs_mounts + smb_mounts }}"

- name: Könyvtárak létrehozása (Csak ha NEM léteznek)
  become: yes
  file:
    path: "{{ item.item.path }}"
    state: directory
    owner: 1000
    group: 1000
    mode: '0775'
  loop: "{{ mount_stat.results }}"
  when: not item.stat.exists 

- name: NFS felcsatolása
  become: yes
  mount:
    path: "{{ item.path }}"
    src: "{{ item.src }}"
    fstype: nfs
    opts: "{{ item.opts }}"
    state: mounted
  loop: "{{ nfs_mounts | default([]) }}"

- name: SMB felcsatolása
  become: yes
  mount:
    path: "{{ item.path }}"
    src: "{{ item.src }}"
    fstype: cifs
    opts: "{{ item.opts }}"
    state: mounted
  loop: "{{ smb_mounts | default([]) }}"

--- FILE: ./13-Infrastructure_as_Code_(IaC)/ansible/roles/system_update/tasks/main.yml ---
# 1. APT LOCK FELOLDÁS
- name: Háttérben futó update folyamatok kinyírása
  shell: |
    systemctl stop apt-daily.service apt-daily.timer || true
    systemctl stop apt-daily-upgrade.service apt-daily-upgrade.timer || true
    systemctl stop unattended-upgrades.service || true
    killall apt apt-get dpkg 2>/dev/null || true
    rm -f /var/lib/dpkg/lock*
    rm -f /var/lib/apt/lists/lock
    rm -f /var/cache/apt/archives/lock
    dpkg --configure -a
  become: yes
  changed_when: false

# 2. RENDSZER FRISSÍTÉS
- name: Rendszer frissítés (Upgrade dist)
  apt:
    upgrade: dist
    autoremove: yes
    force_apt_get: yes
  environment:
    DEBIAN_FRONTEND: noninteractive
  async: 300
  poll: 5
  register: upgrade_output
  become: yes

# 3. TISZTÍTÁS
- name: Felesleges csomagok és cache törlése
  shell: |
    apt-get autoremove --purge -y
    apt-get clean
    journalctl --vacuum-time=1d
  become: yes
  changed_when: false

# 4. REBOOT ELLENŐRZÉS
- name: Reboot ellenőrzése
  stat:
    path: /var/run/reboot-required
  register: reboot_required
  notify: "Rendszer ujrainditasa"

--- FILE: ./13-Infrastructure_as_Code_(IaC)/kubernetes/apps/access/guacamole/configmap-initdb.yaml ---
apiVersion: v1
kind: ConfigMap
metadata:
  name: guacamole-db-init
  namespace: access
data:
  initdb.sql: |
    -- Connection group types
    CREATE TYPE guacamole_connection_group_type AS ENUM(
        'ORGANIZATIONAL',
        'BALANCING'
    );

    -- Entity types
    CREATE TYPE guacamole_entity_type AS ENUM(
        'USER',
        'USER_GROUP'
    );

    -- Object permission types
    CREATE TYPE guacamole_object_permission_type AS ENUM(
        'READ',
        'UPDATE',
        'DELETE',
        'ADMINISTER'
    );

    -- System permission types
    CREATE TYPE guacamole_system_permission_type AS ENUM(
        'CREATE_CONNECTION',
        'CREATE_CONNECTION_GROUP',
        'CREATE_SHARING_PROFILE',
        'CREATE_USER',
        'CREATE_USER_GROUP',
        'AUDIT',
        'ADMINISTER'
    );

    -- Guacamole proxy (guacd) encryption methods
    CREATE TYPE guacamole_proxy_encryption_method AS ENUM(
        'NONE',
        'SSL'
    );

    -- Table of connection groups. Each connection group has a name.
    CREATE TABLE guacamole_connection_group (
      connection_group_id   serial       NOT NULL,
      parent_id             integer,
      connection_group_name varchar(128) NOT NULL,
      type                  guacamole_connection_group_type
                            NOT NULL DEFAULT 'ORGANIZATIONAL',
      max_connections           integer,
      max_connections_per_user integer,
      enable_session_affinity  boolean NOT NULL DEFAULT FALSE,
      PRIMARY KEY (connection_group_id),
      CONSTRAINT connection_group_name_parent
        UNIQUE (connection_group_name, parent_id),
      CONSTRAINT guacamole_connection_group_ibfk_1
        FOREIGN KEY (parent_id)
        REFERENCES guacamole_connection_group (connection_group_id)
        ON DELETE CASCADE
    );

    CREATE INDEX guacamole_connection_group_parent_id
        ON guacamole_connection_group(parent_id);

    -- Table of connections. Each connection has a name, protocol, and
    -- associated set of parameters.
    CREATE TABLE guacamole_connection (
      connection_id       serial       NOT NULL,
      connection_name      varchar(128) NOT NULL,
      parent_id            integer,
      protocol             varchar(32)  NOT NULL,
      max_connections           integer,
      max_connections_per_user integer,
      connection_weight        integer,
      failover_only            boolean NOT NULL DEFAULT FALSE,
      proxy_port              integer,
      proxy_hostname          varchar(512),
      proxy_encryption_method guacamole_proxy_encryption_method,
      PRIMARY KEY (connection_id),
      CONSTRAINT connection_name_parent
        UNIQUE (connection_name, parent_id),
      CONSTRAINT guacamole_connection_ibfk_1
        FOREIGN KEY (parent_id)
        REFERENCES guacamole_connection_group (connection_group_id)
        ON DELETE CASCADE
    );

    CREATE INDEX guacamole_connection_parent_id
        ON guacamole_connection(parent_id);

    CREATE TABLE guacamole_entity (
      entity_id     serial                  NOT NULL,
      name          varchar(128)            NOT NULL,
      type          guacamole_entity_type   NOT NULL,
      PRIMARY KEY (entity_id),
      CONSTRAINT guacamole_entity_name_scope
        UNIQUE (type, name)
    );

    CREATE TABLE guacamole_user (
      user_id       serial       NOT NULL,
      entity_id     integer      NOT NULL,
      password_hash bytea        NOT NULL,
      password_salt bytea,
      password_date timestamptz  NOT NULL,
      disabled      boolean      NOT NULL DEFAULT FALSE,
      expired       boolean      NOT NULL DEFAULT FALSE,
      access_window_start    time,
      access_window_end      time,
      valid_from  date,
      valid_until date,
      timezone varchar(64),
      full_name           varchar(256),
      email_address       varchar(256),
      organization        varchar(256),
      organizational_role varchar(256),
      PRIMARY KEY (user_id),
      CONSTRAINT guacamole_user_single_entity
        UNIQUE (entity_id),
      CONSTRAINT guacamole_user_entity
        FOREIGN KEY (entity_id)
        REFERENCES guacamole_entity (entity_id)
        ON DELETE CASCADE
    );

    CREATE TABLE guacamole_user_group (
      user_group_id serial      NOT NULL,
      entity_id     integer     NOT NULL,
      disabled      boolean     NOT NULL DEFAULT FALSE,
      PRIMARY KEY (user_group_id),
      CONSTRAINT guacamole_user_group_single_entity
        UNIQUE (entity_id),
      CONSTRAINT guacamole_user_group_entity
        FOREIGN KEY (entity_id)
        REFERENCES guacamole_entity (entity_id)
        ON DELETE CASCADE
    );

    CREATE TABLE guacamole_user_group_member (
      user_group_id    integer       NOT NULL,
      member_entity_id integer       NOT NULL,
      PRIMARY KEY (user_group_id, member_entity_id),
      CONSTRAINT guacamole_user_group_member_parent
        FOREIGN KEY (user_group_id)
        REFERENCES guacamole_user_group (user_group_id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
      CONSTRAINT guacamole_user_group_member_entity
        FOREIGN KEY (member_entity_id)
        REFERENCES guacamole_entity (entity_id) ON DELETE CASCADE
    );

    CREATE TABLE guacamole_sharing_profile (
      sharing_profile_id    serial       NOT NULL,
      sharing_profile_name  varchar(128) NOT NULL,
      primary_connection_id integer      NOT NULL,
      PRIMARY KEY (sharing_profile_id),
      CONSTRAINT sharing_profile_name_primary
        UNIQUE (sharing_profile_name, primary_connection_id),
      CONSTRAINT guacamole_sharing_profile_ibfk_1
        FOREIGN KEY (primary_connection_id)
        REFERENCES guacamole_connection (connection_id)
        ON DELETE CASCADE
    );

    CREATE INDEX guacamole_sharing_profile_primary_connection_id
        ON guacamole_sharing_profile(primary_connection_id);

    CREATE TABLE guacamole_connection_parameter (
      connection_id   integer       NOT NULL,
      parameter_name  varchar(128)  NOT NULL,
      parameter_value varchar(4096) NOT NULL,
      PRIMARY KEY (connection_id,parameter_name),
      CONSTRAINT guacamole_connection_parameter_ibfk_1
        FOREIGN KEY (connection_id)
        REFERENCES guacamole_connection (connection_id) ON DELETE CASCADE
    );

    CREATE INDEX guacamole_connection_parameter_connection_id
        ON guacamole_connection_parameter(connection_id);

    CREATE TABLE guacamole_sharing_profile_parameter (
      sharing_profile_id integer       NOT NULL,
      parameter_name     varchar(128)  NOT NULL,
      parameter_value    varchar(4096) NOT NULL,
      PRIMARY KEY (sharing_profile_id, parameter_name),
      CONSTRAINT guacamole_sharing_profile_parameter_ibfk_1
        FOREIGN KEY (sharing_profile_id)
        REFERENCES guacamole_sharing_profile (sharing_profile_id) ON DELETE CASCADE
    );

    CREATE INDEX guacamole_sharing_profile_parameter_sharing_profile_id
        ON guacamole_sharing_profile_parameter(sharing_profile_id);

    CREATE TABLE guacamole_user_attribute (
      user_id          integer       NOT NULL,
      attribute_name  varchar(128)  NOT NULL,
      attribute_value varchar(4096) NOT NULL,
      PRIMARY KEY (user_id, attribute_name),
      CONSTRAINT guacamole_user_attribute_ibfk_1
        FOREIGN KEY (user_id)
        REFERENCES guacamole_user (user_id) ON DELETE CASCADE
    );

    CREATE INDEX guacamole_user_attribute_user_id
        ON guacamole_user_attribute(user_id);

    CREATE TABLE guacamole_user_group_attribute (
      user_group_id   integer       NOT NULL,
      attribute_name  varchar(128)  NOT NULL,
      attribute_value varchar(4096) NOT NULL,
      PRIMARY KEY (user_group_id, attribute_name),
      CONSTRAINT guacamole_user_group_attribute_ibfk_1
        FOREIGN KEY (user_group_id)
        REFERENCES guacamole_user_group (user_group_id) ON DELETE CASCADE
    );

    CREATE INDEX guacamole_user_group_attribute_user_group_id
        ON guacamole_user_group_attribute(user_group_id);

    CREATE TABLE guacamole_connection_attribute (
      connection_id   integer       NOT NULL,
      attribute_name  varchar(128)  NOT NULL,
      attribute_value varchar(4096) NOT NULL,
      PRIMARY KEY (connection_id, attribute_name),
      CONSTRAINT guacamole_connection_attribute_ibfk_1
        FOREIGN KEY (connection_id)
        REFERENCES guacamole_connection (connection_id) ON DELETE CASCADE
    );

    CREATE INDEX guacamole_connection_attribute_connection_id
        ON guacamole_connection_attribute(connection_id);

    CREATE TABLE guacamole_connection_group_attribute (
      connection_group_id integer       NOT NULL,
      attribute_name      varchar(128)  NOT NULL,
      attribute_value     varchar(4096) NOT NULL,
      PRIMARY KEY (connection_group_id, attribute_name),
      CONSTRAINT guacamole_connection_group_attribute_ibfk_1
        FOREIGN KEY (connection_group_id)
        REFERENCES guacamole_connection_group (connection_group_id) ON DELETE CASCADE
    );

    CREATE INDEX guacamole_connection_group_attribute_connection_group_id
        ON guacamole_connection_group_attribute(connection_group_id);

    CREATE TABLE guacamole_sharing_profile_attribute (
      sharing_profile_id integer       NOT NULL,
      attribute_name     varchar(128)  NOT NULL,
      attribute_value    varchar(4096) NOT NULL,
      PRIMARY KEY (sharing_profile_id, attribute_name),
      CONSTRAINT guacamole_sharing_profile_attribute_ibfk_1
        FOREIGN KEY (sharing_profile_id)
        REFERENCES guacamole_sharing_profile (sharing_profile_id) ON DELETE CASCADE
    );

    CREATE INDEX guacamole_sharing_profile_attribute_sharing_profile_id
        ON guacamole_sharing_profile_attribute(sharing_profile_id);

    CREATE TABLE guacamole_connection_permission (
      entity_id     integer NOT NULL,
      connection_id integer NOT NULL,
      permission    guacamole_object_permission_type NOT NULL,
      PRIMARY KEY (entity_id, connection_id, permission),
      CONSTRAINT guacamole_connection_permission_ibfk_1
        FOREIGN KEY (connection_id)
        REFERENCES guacamole_connection (connection_id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
      CONSTRAINT guacamole_connection_permission_entity
        FOREIGN KEY (entity_id)
        REFERENCES guacamole_entity (entity_id) ON DELETE CASCADE
    );

    CREATE INDEX guacamole_connection_permission_connection_id
        ON guacamole_connection_permission(connection_id);

    CREATE INDEX guacamole_connection_permission_entity_id
        ON guacamole_connection_permission(entity_id);

    CREATE TABLE guacamole_connection_group_permission (
      entity_id           integer NOT NULL,
      connection_group_id integer NOT NULL,
      permission          guacamole_object_permission_type NOT NULL,
      PRIMARY KEY (entity_id, connection_group_id, permission),
      CONSTRAINT guacamole_connection_group_permission_ibfk_1
        FOREIGN KEY (connection_group_id)
        REFERENCES guacamole_connection_group (connection_group_id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
      CONSTRAINT guacamole_connection_group_permission_entity
        FOREIGN KEY (entity_id)
        REFERENCES guacamole_entity (entity_id) ON DELETE CASCADE
    );

    CREATE INDEX guacamole_connection_group_permission_connection_group_id
        ON guacamole_connection_group_permission(connection_group_id);

    CREATE INDEX guacamole_connection_group_permission_entity_id
        ON guacamole_connection_group_permission(entity_id);

    CREATE TABLE guacamole_sharing_profile_permission (
      entity_id          integer NOT NULL,
      sharing_profile_id integer NOT NULL,
      permission          guacamole_object_permission_type NOT NULL,
      PRIMARY KEY (entity_id, sharing_profile_id, permission),
      CONSTRAINT guacamole_sharing_profile_permission_ibfk_1
        FOREIGN KEY (sharing_profile_id)
        REFERENCES guacamole_sharing_profile (sharing_profile_id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
      CONSTRAINT guacamole_sharing_profile_permission_entity
        FOREIGN KEY (entity_id)
        REFERENCES guacamole_entity (entity_id) ON DELETE CASCADE
    );

    CREATE INDEX guacamole_sharing_profile_permission_sharing_profile_id
        ON guacamole_sharing_profile_permission(sharing_profile_id);

    CREATE INDEX guacamole_sharing_profile_permission_entity_id
        ON guacamole_sharing_profile_permission(entity_id);

    CREATE TABLE guacamole_system_permission (
      entity_id  integer NOT NULL,
      permission guacamole_system_permission_type NOT NULL,
      PRIMARY KEY (entity_id, permission),
      CONSTRAINT guacamole_system_permission_entity
        FOREIGN KEY (entity_id)
        REFERENCES guacamole_entity (entity_id) ON DELETE CASCADE
    );

    CREATE INDEX guacamole_system_permission_entity_id
        ON guacamole_system_permission(entity_id);

    CREATE TABLE guacamole_user_permission (
      entity_id         integer NOT NULL,
      affected_user_id integer NOT NULL,
      permission        guacamole_object_permission_type NOT NULL,
      PRIMARY KEY (entity_id, affected_user_id, permission),
      CONSTRAINT guacamole_user_permission_ibfk_1
        FOREIGN KEY (affected_user_id)
        REFERENCES guacamole_user (user_id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
      CONSTRAINT guacamole_user_permission_entity
        FOREIGN KEY (entity_id)
        REFERENCES guacamole_entity (entity_id) ON DELETE CASCADE
    );

    CREATE INDEX guacamole_user_permission_affected_user_id
        ON guacamole_user_permission(affected_user_id);

    CREATE INDEX guacamole_user_permission_entity_id
        ON guacamole_user_permission(entity_id);

    CREATE TABLE guacamole_user_group_permission (
      entity_id               integer NOT NULL,
      affected_user_group_id integer NOT NULL,
      permission               guacamole_object_permission_type NOT NULL,
      PRIMARY KEY (entity_id, affected_user_group_id, permission),
      CONSTRAINT guacamole_user_group_permission_affected_user_group
        FOREIGN KEY (affected_user_group_id)
        REFERENCES guacamole_user_group (user_group_id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
      CONSTRAINT guacamole_user_group_permission_entity
        FOREIGN KEY (entity_id)
        REFERENCES guacamole_entity (entity_id) ON DELETE CASCADE
    );

    CREATE INDEX guacamole_user_group_permission_affected_user_group_id
        ON guacamole_user_group_permission(affected_user_group_id);

    CREATE INDEX guacamole_user_group_permission_entity_id
        ON guacamole_user_group_permission(entity_id);

    CREATE TABLE guacamole_connection_history (
      history_id           serial       NOT NULL,
      user_id              integer      DEFAULT NULL,
      username              varchar(128) NOT NULL,
      remote_host          varchar(256) DEFAULT NULL,
      connection_id        integer      DEFAULT NULL,
      connection_name      varchar(128) NOT NULL,
      sharing_profile_id   integer      DEFAULT NULL,
      sharing_profile_name varchar(128) DEFAULT NULL,
      start_date           timestamptz  NOT NULL,
      end_date             timestamptz  DEFAULT NULL,
      PRIMARY KEY (history_id),
      CONSTRAINT guacamole_connection_history_ibfk_1
        FOREIGN KEY (user_id)
        REFERENCES guacamole_user (user_id) ON DELETE SET NULL,
      CONSTRAINT guacamole_connection_history_ibfk_2
        FOREIGN KEY (connection_id)
        REFERENCES guacamole_connection (connection_id) ON DELETE SET NULL,
      CONSTRAINT guacamole_connection_history_ibfk_3
        FOREIGN KEY (sharing_profile_id)
        REFERENCES guacamole_sharing_profile (sharing_profile_id) ON DELETE SET NULL
    );

    CREATE INDEX guacamole_connection_history_user_id
        ON guacamole_connection_history(user_id);
    CREATE INDEX guacamole_connection_history_connection_id
        ON guacamole_connection_history(connection_id);
    CREATE INDEX guacamole_connection_history_sharing_profile_id
        ON guacamole_connection_history(sharing_profile_id);
    CREATE INDEX guacamole_connection_history_start_date
        ON guacamole_connection_history(start_date);
    CREATE INDEX guacamole_connection_history_end_date
        ON guacamole_connection_history(end_date);
    CREATE INDEX guacamole_connection_history_connection_id_start_date
        ON guacamole_connection_history(connection_id, start_date);

    CREATE TABLE guacamole_user_history (
      history_id           serial       NOT NULL,
      user_id              integer      DEFAULT NULL,
      username              varchar(128) NOT NULL,
      remote_host          varchar(256) DEFAULT NULL,
      start_date           timestamptz  NOT NULL,
      end_date             timestamptz  DEFAULT NULL,
      PRIMARY KEY (history_id),
      CONSTRAINT guacamole_user_history_ibfk_1
        FOREIGN KEY (user_id)
        REFERENCES guacamole_user (user_id) ON DELETE SET NULL
    );

    CREATE INDEX guacamole_user_history_user_id
        ON guacamole_user_history(user_id);
    CREATE INDEX guacamole_user_history_start_date
        ON guacamole_user_history(start_date);
    CREATE INDEX guacamole_user_history_end_date
        ON guacamole_user_history(end_date);
    CREATE INDEX guacamole_user_history_user_id_start_date
        ON guacamole_user_history(user_id, start_date);

    CREATE TABLE guacamole_user_password_history (
      password_history_id serial  NOT NULL,
      user_id              integer NOT NULL,
      password_hash bytea        NOT NULL,
      password_salt bytea,
      password_date timestamptz  NOT NULL,
      PRIMARY KEY (password_history_id),
      CONSTRAINT guacamole_user_password_history_ibfk_1
        FOREIGN KEY (user_id)
        REFERENCES guacamole_user (user_id) ON DELETE CASCADE
    );

    CREATE INDEX guacamole_user_password_history_user_id
        ON guacamole_user_password_history(user_id);

    INSERT INTO guacamole_entity (name, type) VALUES ('guacadmin', 'USER');
    INSERT INTO guacamole_user (entity_id, password_hash, password_salt, password_date)
    SELECT
        entity_id,
        decode('CA458A7D494E3BE824F5E1E175A1556C0F8EEF2C2D7DF3633BEC4A29C4411960', 'hex'),
        decode('FE24ADC5E11E2B25288D1704ABE67A79E342ECC26064CE69C5B3177795A82264', 'hex'),
        CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
    FROM guacamole_entity WHERE name = 'guacadmin' AND guacamole_entity.type = 'USER';

    INSERT INTO guacamole_system_permission (entity_id, permission)
    SELECT entity_id, permission::guacamole_system_permission_type
    FROM (
        VALUES
            ('guacadmin', 'CREATE_CONNECTION'),
            ('guacadmin', 'CREATE_CONNECTION_GROUP'),
            ('guacadmin', 'CREATE_SHARING_PROFILE'),
            ('guacadmin', 'CREATE_USER'),
            ('guacadmin', 'CREATE_USER_GROUP'),
            ('guacadmin', 'ADMINISTER')
    ) permissions (username, permission)
    JOIN guacamole_entity ON permissions.username = guacamole_entity.name AND guacamole_entity.type = 'USER';

    INSERT INTO guacamole_user_permission (entity_id, affected_user_id, permission)
    SELECT guacamole_entity.entity_id, guacamole_user.user_id, permission::guacamole_object_permission_type
    FROM (
        VALUES
            ('guacadmin', 'guacadmin', 'READ'),
            ('guacadmin', 'guacadmin', 'UPDATE'),
            ('guacadmin', 'guacadmin', 'ADMINISTER')
    ) permissions (username, affected_username, permission)
    JOIN guacamole_entity          ON permissions.username = guacamole_entity.name AND guacamole_entity.type = 'USER'
    JOIN guacamole_entity affected ON permissions.affected_username = affected.name AND guacamole_entity.type = 'USER'
    JOIN guacamole_user            ON guacamole_user.entity_id = affected.entity_id;


--- FILE: ./13-Infrastructure_as_Code_(IaC)/kubernetes/apps/access/guacamole/database.yaml ---
apiVersion: apps/v1
kind: StatefulSet
metadata:
  name: guacamole-db
  namespace: access
spec:
  serviceName: "guacamole-db"
  replicas: 1
  selector:
    matchLabels:
      app: guacamole-db
  template:
    metadata:
      labels:
        app: guacamole-db
    spec:
      containers:
      - name: postgres
        image: postgres:15.18
        env:
          - name: POSTGRES_DB
            value: "guacamole_db"
          - name: POSTGRES_USER
            value: "guacamole_user"
          - name: POSTGRES_PASSWORD
            valueFrom:
              secretKeyRef:
                name: guacamole-secrets
                key: POSTGRES_PASSWORD
        ports:
          - containerPort: 5432
        volumeMounts:
          - name: db-data
            mountPath: /var/lib/postgresql/data
          - name: init-script
            mountPath: /docker-entrypoint-initdb.d/initdb.sql
            subPath: initdb.sql
      volumes:
        - name: db-data
          hostPath:
            path: /opt/app-data/access-stack/guacamole/db
            type: DirectoryOrCreate
        - name: init-script
          configMap:
            name: guacamole-db-init
---
apiVersion: v1
kind: Service
metadata:
  name: guacamole-db
  namespace: access
spec:
  selector:
    app: guacamole-db
  ports:
    - port: 5432
      targetPort: 5432

              value: "preferred_username"
            - name: OPENID_GROUPS_CLAIM

      template:

            runAsUser: 1000
          nodeSelector:
            kubernetes.io/hostname: k3s-server-01-225
          containers:
          - name: renovate
            image: renovate/renovate:43.216
            env:
            - name: RENOVATE_PLATFORM
              value: "github"
            - name: RENOVATE_TOKEN
              valueFrom:
                secretKeyRef:
                  name: renovate-secrets
                  key: RENOVATE_TOKEN
            - name: RENOVATE_REPOSITORIES
              value: '["torokrolf/homelab-infra"]'
            - name: RENOVATE_AUTODISCOVER
              value: "false"
            - name: LOG_LEVEL
              value: "debug"
            - name: RENOVATE_CACHE_DIR
              value: "/tmp/renovate/cache"
            volumeMounts:
            - name: workdir
              mountPath: /tmp/renovate

          - name: workdir

kind: Deployment
metadata:
  name: qbittorrent

  replicas: 1

    matchLabels:
      app: qbittorrent
  template:
    metadata:

        app: qbittorrent

              value: Europe/Budapest
            - name: WEBUI_PORT
              value: "8080"
            - name: QBT_Preferences__WebUI__AuthSubnetWhitelistEnabled
              value: "false"  
            - name: QBT_Preferences__WebUI__AuthSubnetWhitelist
              value: ""      
            - name: QBT_Preferences__WebUI__LocalHostAuthenticationEnabled
              value: "true"   
            - name: QBT_Preferences__WebUI__HostHeaderValidation
              value: "true"   
          volumeMounts:
            - name: config
              mountPath: /config
            - name: downloads
              mountPath: /data

--- FILE: ./13-Infrastructure_as_Code_(IaC)/kubernetes/apps/monitoring/grafana/deployment.yaml ---
apiVersion: apps/v1
kind: Deployment
metadata:
  name: grafana
  namespace: monitoring
spec:
  replicas: 1
  selector:
    matchLabels:
      app: grafana
  template:
    metadata:
      labels:
        app: grafana
    spec:
      nodeSelector:
        kubernetes.io/hostname: k3s-server-01-225
      securityContext:
        fsGroup: 472
        runAsUser: 472
        runAsGroup: 472
      initContainers:
        - name: fix-permissions
          image: busybox
          command: ["sh", "-c", "chown -R 472:472 /var/lib/grafana"]
          securityContext:
            runAsUser: 0
          volumeMounts:
            - name: storage
              mountPath: /var/lib/grafana
      containers:
        - name: grafana
          image: grafana/grafana:13.0.2
          ports:
            - containerPort: 3000
          env:
            - name: GF_AUTH_GENERIC_OAUTH_ENABLED
              value: "true"
            - name: GF_AUTH_GENERIC_OAUTH_NAME
              value: "Authentik"
            - name: GF_AUTH_GENERIC_OAUTH_CLIENT_ID
              valueFrom:
                secretKeyRef:
                  name: grafana-secrets
                  key: GF_AUTH_GENERIC_OAUTH_CLIENT_ID
            - name: GF_AUTH_GENERIC_OAUTH_CLIENT_SECRET
              valueFrom:
                secretKeyRef:
                  name: grafana-secrets
                  key: GF_AUTH_GENERIC_OAUTH_CLIENT_SECRET
            - name: GF_AUTH_GENERIC_OAUTH_SCOPES
              value: "openid profile email"
            - name: GF_AUTH_GENERIC_OAUTH_AUTH_URL
              value: "https://authentik.trkrolf.com/application/o/authorize/"
            - name: GF_AUTH_GENERIC_OAUTH_TOKEN_URL
              value: "https://authentik.trkrolf.com/application/o/token/"
            - name: GF_AUTH_GENERIC_OAUTH_API_URL
              value: "https://authentik.trkrolf.com/application/o/userinfo/"
            - name: GF_AUTH_GENERIC_OAUTH_AUTO_LOGIN
              value: "true"
            - name: GF_SERVER_ROOT_URL
              value: "https://grafana.trkrolf.com"
            - name: GF_SERVER_DOMAIN
              value: "grafana.trkrolf.com"
            - name: GF_AUTH_GENERIC_OAUTH_ROLE_ATTRIBUTE_PATH
              value: "contains(groups, 'Admins') && 'Admin' || 'Viewer'"
            - name: GF_AUTH_GENERIC_OAUTH_ALLOW_ASSIGN_GRAFANA_ADMIN
              value: "true"

          volumeMounts:
            - name: storage
              mountPath: /var/lib/grafana
      volumes:
        - name: storage

--- FILE: ./13-Infrastructure_as_Code_(IaC)/kubernetes/apps/storage/nextcloud/app-deployment.yaml ---
apiVersion: apps/v1
kind: Deployment
metadata:
  name: nextcloud-app
  namespace: storage
spec:
  replicas: 1
  selector:
    matchLabels:
      app: nextcloud-app
  template:
    metadata:
      labels:
        app: nextcloud-app
    spec:
      containers:
        - name: nextcloud
          image: nextcloud:33.0.5
          env:
            - name: MYSQL_PASSWORD
              valueFrom:
                secretKeyRef:
                  name: nextcloud-db-secrets
                  key: MYSQL_PASSWORD
            - name: OIDC_CLIENT_ID
              valueFrom:
                secretKeyRef:
                  name: nextcloud-db-secrets
                  key: CLIENT_ID
            - name: OIDC_CLIENT_SECRET
              valueFrom:
                secretKeyRef:
                  name: nextcloud-db-secrets
                  key: CLIENT_SECRET
            - name: MYSQL_DATABASE
              value: "nextcloud_db"
            - name: MYSQL_USER
              value: "rolf"
            - name: MYSQL_HOST
              value: "nextcloud-db"
          ports:
            - containerPort: 80
          volumeMounts:
            - name: app-data
              mountPath: /var/www/html/data
            - name: app-config
              mountPath: /var/www/html/config
          lifecycle:
            postStart:
              exec:
                command:
                  - "/bin/sh"
                  - "-c"
                  - |
                    sleep 30;
                    
                    # 1. Alapvető rendszerbeállítások (Ezek oldották meg a hibát!)
                    runuser -u www-data -- php occ config:system:set allow_local_remote_servers --value="true" --type=bool;
                    runuser -u www-data -- php occ config:system:set overwrite.cli.url --value="https://nextcloud.trkrolf.com";
                    runuser -u www-data -- php occ config:system:set overwriteprotocol --value="https";
                    
                    # 2. OIDC App telepítés/engedélyezés
                    runuser -u www-data -- php occ app:install user_oidc || runuser -u www-data -- php occ app:enable user_oidc;
                    
                    # 3. Provider konfiguráció
                    runuser -u www-data -- php occ user_oidc:provider authentik \
                      --clientid="$OIDC_CLIENT_ID" \
                      --clientsecret="$OIDC_CLIENT_SECRET" \
                      --discoveryuri="https://authentik.trkrolf.com/application/o/nextcloud/.well-known/openid-configuration" \
                      --scope="openid profile email groups";
                    
                    # 4. Redirect URI és felület finomhangolás
                    runuser -u www-data -- php occ config:app:set user_oidc provider-authentik-redirectUrl --value="https://nextcloud.trkrolf.com/index.php/apps/user_oidc/code";
                    runuser -u www-data -- php occ config:app:set user_oidc show_alternative_logins --value="1";
                    runuser -u www-data -- php occ config:system:set allow_user_to_back_to_login_after_logout --value="true" --type=bool;

      volumes:
        - name: app-data
          hostPath:
            path: /opt/app-data/storage-stack/nextcloud/data
            type: DirectoryOrCreate
        - name: app-config
          hostPath:
            path: /opt/app-data/storage-stack/nextcloud/config
            type: DirectoryOrCreate
